<div class="wp-block-stackable-column stk-block-column stk-column stk-block stk-aeaf593" data-v="4" data-block-id="aeaf593"><div class="stk-column-wrapper stk-block-column__content stk-container stk-aeaf593-container stk--no-background stk--no-padding"><div class="stk-block-content stk-inner-blocks stk-aeaf593-inner-blocks">
<div class="wp-block-stackable-heading stk-block-heading stk-block-heading--v2 stk-block stk-67573b1" id="what-sets-our-pop-workplace-preschool-in-outram-apart" data-block-id="67573b1"><h2 class="stk-block-heading__text has-text-color">What Sets our POP Workplace Preschool in Outram Apart</h2></div>



<p>The <a href="https://www.littleskoolhouse.com/">Little Skool-House</a> preschool in Outram is located at the Outram Community Hospital, a major institution in Singapore housed within SingHealth Tower in Hospital Boulevard. Placing value on the importance of nurturing a child’s mind, our centre features an environment conducive to our <a href="https://www.littleskoolhouse.com/our-difference/" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">award-winning educators</a> engaging young minds</p>



<p>Being the<a href="https://www.littleskoolhouse.com/our-difference/" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener"> chosen preschool by top institutions</a>, our POP workplace centre in Outram Community Hospital is the preferred preschool for employees of our workplace centre partner in Outram. Established to provide working parents with a safe place for their children during working hours, our centre is a convenient option for parents working in the area.</p>



<div class="wp-block-stackable-text stk-block-text stk-block stk-62357a7" data-block-id="62357a7"><p class="stk-block-text__text">The Little Skool-House kindergarten in Outram has been awarded the Spark certification by ECDA and Healthy Pre-Schools (HPS) Accreditation in Singapore. We create a safe and nurturing learning environment that teaches kids the importance of proper nutrition and staying active.</p></div>
</div></div></div>

<div class="wp-block-stackable-heading stk-block-heading stk-block-heading--v2 stk-block stk-51e1ed1" id="programmes-offered" data-block-id="51e1ed1"><h2 class="stk-block-heading__text has-text-color">Programmes Offered</h2></div>



<div class="wp-block-stackable-text stk-block-text stk-block stk-140ca50" data-block-id="140ca50"><p class="stk-block-text__text">We run a full-day programme for preschoolers, following a pedagogy based on clinical research on child development and education has led to 93% of Little Skool-House preschoolers being <a href="https://www.littleskoolhouse.com/our-difference/" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">Highly Proficient in both English and Mandarin</a>. We also offer a range of <a href="https://www.littleskoolhouse.com/curriculum/enrichment-programmes/" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">enrichment programmes</a> for more holistic development.</p></div>

<div class="wp-block-stackable-column stk-block-column stk-column stk-block stk-c3da87e stk-block-accordion__content" data-v="4" data-block-id="c3da87e"><div class="stk-column-wrapper stk-block-column__content stk-container stk-c3da87e-container stk--no-background stk--no-padding"><div class="stk-block-content stk-inner-blocks stk-c3da87e-inner-blocks">
<div class="wp-block-stackable-text stk-block-text stk-block stk-2592a60" data-block-id="2592a60"><p class="stk-block-text__text">At the Little Skool-House kindergarten in Outram, we offer full-day programmes for preschoolers in Singapore, aged between 18 months and 6-years old. Our pedagogy based on clinical research on child development and education has led to 93% of Little Skool-House preschoolers being Highly Proficient in both English and Mandarin. In addition, the Little Skool-House kindergarten in Outram and all around Singapore, offers a range of enrichment programmes for a more holistic development.</p></div>

<div class="wp-block-stackable-subtitle stk-block-subtitle stk-block stk-9c55831" data-block-id="9c55831"><p class="stk-block-subtitle__text stk-subtitle has-text-color has-text-align-left">Principal</p></div>



<div class="wp-block-stackable-subtitle stk-block-subtitle stk-block stk-6e8e325" data-block-id="6e8e325"><p class="stk-block-subtitle__text stk-subtitle has-text-color has-text-align-left">Diploma in Kindergarten Education – Teaching</p></div>
</div></div></div></div>



<div class="wp-block-stackable-text stk-block-text stk-block stk-2f6aa04" data-block-id="2f6aa04"><p class="stk-block-text__text">Marie believes in creating a “Home Away from Home”. This means providing a positive and safe environment for children to explore and learn, unleash their potential and prepare them for life. She believes that this vision can be achieved through close partnerships with teachers, families and the community. In her free time, Marie enjoys singing and playing the piano with her husband and children.</p></div>

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>Within the Little Skool-House network of centres, 14 of them operate as Partner Operator (POP) centres under the Partner Operator scheme governed by ECDA. This programme aims to improve accessibility, affordability and quality of childcare and infant care services for working parents. 12 of these centres operate on the premises of our partner employer. However, in all other aspects, our POP centres are consistent with all other Little Skool-House centres in the delivery of programmes and curriculum.</p>
